og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">There are so many ways we can build React apps and ship for production. One way is to build React with NodeJS or Java and another way is to build the React and serve that static content with NGINX web server. With Java we have to deal with the server code as well, for example, you need to load index.html page with java.</p><p id="f733" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">In this post, we will see the details and implementation with Java. We will go through step by step with an example.</p><ul class=""><li id="e328" class="oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on pa op oq or pb ot ou ov pc ox oy oz pd pe pf bj"><strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">Introduction</em></strong></li><li id="35e3" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj"><strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">Prerequisites</em></strong></li><li id="bfe6" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj"><strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">Example Project</em></strong></li><li id="f8e6" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj"><strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">How To Build and Develop The Project</em></strong></li><li id="67ba" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj"><strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">How To Build For Production</em></strong></li><li id="d7d6" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj"><strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">Summary</em></strong></li><li id="ae42" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj"><strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">Conclusion</em></strong></li></ul><h1 id="259e" class="pm pn hc be po pp pq hy pr ps pt ib pu pv pw px py pz qa qb qc qd qe qf qg qh bj">Introduction</h1><p id="2414" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on qk op oq or ql ot ou ov qm ox oy oz gv bj">React is a javascript library for building web apps and it doesn’t load itself in the browser. We need some kind of mechanism that loads the index.html (single page) of React with all the dependencies(CSS and js files) in the browser. In this case, we are using java as the webserver which loads React assets and accepts any API calls from the React app.</p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt nl nm paragraph-image"><div role="button" Java</strong></figcaption></figure><p id="1776" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">If you look at the above diagram all the web requests without the <strong class="og hd">/api </strong>will go to React router. All the paths that contain <strong class="og hd">/api </strong>will be handled by the Apache Tomcat container.</p></div></div></div><div class="ab ca qo qp qq qr" role="separator"><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu"></span></div><div class="gv gw gx gy gz"><div class="ab ca"><div class="ch bg fx fy fz ga"><h1 id="ba7b" class="pm pn hc be po pp qw hy pr ps qx ib pu pv qy px py pz qz qb qc qd ra qf qg qh bj">Prerequisites</h1><p id="336d" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on qk op oq or ql ot ou ov qm ox oy oz gv bj">There are some prerequisites for this article. You need to have java installed on your laptop and how http works. If you want to practice and run this on your laptop you need to have these on your laptop.</p><ul class=""><li id="fe33" class="oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on pa op oq or pb ot ou ov pc ox oy oz pd pe pf bj"><a class="af od" href="https://www.java.com/en/download/" rel="noopener ugc nofollow" target="_blank">Java</a></li><li id="00a1" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj App</a></li><li id="abe9" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj"><a class="af od" href="https://code.visualstudio.com/" rel="noopener ugc nofollow" target="_blank">VSCode</a></li><li id="4004" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj"><a class="af od" href="https://www.eclipse.org/ide/" rel="noopener ugc nofollow" target="_blank">Eclipse IDE</a></li><li id="913b" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd qp qq qr" role="separator"><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu"></span></div><div class="gv gw gx gy gz"><div class="ab ca"><div class="ch bg fx fy fz ga"><h1 id="1585" class="pm pn hc be po pp qw hy pr ps qx ib pu pv qy px py pz qz qb qc qd ra qf qg qh bj">Example Project</h1><p id="3ed2" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc project. You can clone it and run it on your machine.</p><pre class="no np nq nr ns rc rd re rf ax rg bj"><span id="2c1e" class="rh pn hc rd b jj ri rj l jy rk">// clone the project<br/>git clone <a class="af od" href="https://github.com/bbachi/react-java-example.git" rel="noopener ugc nofollow" target="_blank">https://github.com/bbachi/react-java-example.git</a></span><span id="e623" class="rh pn hc rd b jj rl rj l jy rk">// Run React on port 3000</span><span id="d65e" class="rh pn hc rd b jj rl rj l jy rk">cd /src/main/ui<br/>npm install<br/>npm start</span><span id="bdfb" class="rh pn hc rd b jj rl rj l jy rk">// Run Java Code on 8080<br/>mvn clean install<br/>java -jar target/users-0.0.2-SNAPSHOT.jar</span></pre></div></div></div><div class="ab ca qo qp qq qr" role="separator"><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu"></span></div><div class="gv gw gx gy gz"><div class="ab ca"><div class="ch bg fx fy fz ga"><h1 id="a9de" class="pm pn hc be po pp qw hy pr ps qx ib pu pv qy px py pz qz qb qc qd ra qf qg qh bj">How To Build and Develop The Project</h1><p id="1354" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on qk op oq or ql ot ou ov qm ox oy oz gv bj">Usually, the way you develop and the way you build and run in production are completely different. Thatswhy, I would like to define two phases: Development phase and Production phase.</p><p id="c137" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">In the development phase, we run the java server and the React app on completely different ports. It’s easier and faster to develop that way. If you look at the following diagram the React app is running on port 3<strong class="og hd">000</strong> with the help of a webpack dev server and the java server is running on port <strong class="og hd">8080</strong>.</p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt nl nm paragraph-image"><div class="nl nm rm"><picture><source Environment</strong></figcaption></figure><h2 id="fdd9" class="rh pn hc be po rn ro dx pr rp rq dz pu on rr rs rt or ru rv rw ov rx ry rz sa bj">Project Structure</h2><p id="149b" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on qk op oq or ql ot ou ov qm ox oy oz gv bj">Let’s understand the project structure for this project. We need to have two completely different folders for java and react. It’s always best practice to have completely different folders for each one. In this way, you will have a clean architecture or any other problems regarding merging any files.</p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt nl nm paragraph-image"><div role="button" tabindex="0" class="nu Structure</strong></figcaption></figure><p id="ef5f" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">If you look at the above project structure, all the React app resides under the <strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">src/main/ui</em></strong> folder and Java code resides under the <strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">src/main/java</em></strong> folder. All the resources are under the folder <strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">/src/main/resources</em></strong> such as properties, static assets, etc</p><h2 id="ee14" class="rh pn hc be po rn ro dx pr rp rq dz pu on rr rs rt or ru rv rw ov rx ry rz sa bj">Java API</h2><p id="1dee" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on qk op oq or ql ot ou ov qm ox oy oz gv bj">We use spring boot and a lot of other tools such as Spring Devtools, Spring Actuator, etc under the spring umbrella. Nowadays almost every application has spring boot and it is an open-source Java-based framework used to create a micro Service. It is developed by the Pivotal Team and is used to build stand-alone and production-ready <strong class="og hd">spring</strong> applications.</p><p id="cfdc" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">We start with Spring initializr and select all the dependencies and generate the zip file.</p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt the eclipse or any other IDE as a Maven project you can see all the dependencies in the <strong class="og hd">pom.xml. </strong>Below is the dependencies section of pom.xml.</p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt"><div class="se jz l fg"><div class="sf sg l"></div></div><figcaption class="oa fc gr nl nm ob oc be b bf z dt"><strong class="al">pom.xml</strong></figcaption></figure><p id="f07e" class="al">controller and the main file</strong></figcaption></figure><h2 id="ab9b" class="rh pn hc be po rn ro dx pr rp rq dz pu on rr rs rt or ru rv rw ov rx ry rz sa bj">Configure H2 Database</h2><p id="b078" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on qk op oq or ql ot ou ov qm ox oy oz gv bj">This H2 Database is for development only. When you build this project for production you can replace it with any database of your choice. You can run this database standalone without your application. We will see how we can configure with spring boot.</p><p id="b117" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">First, we need to add some properties to application.properties file under <strong class="og hd">/src/main/resources</strong></p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt"><div class="se jz l fg"><div class="sf sg l"></div></div><figcaption class="oa fc gr nl nm ob oc be b bf z dt"><strong class="al">application.properties</strong></figcaption></figure><p id="53f4" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">Second, add the below SQL file under the same location.</p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt"><div class="se jz l fg"><div class="sf sg l"></div></div><figcaption class="oa fc gr nl nm ob oc be b bf z dt"><strong class="al">data.sql</strong></figcaption></figure><p id="e1d6" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">Third, start the application, and spring boot creates this table on startup. Once the application is started you can go to this URL <a class="af od" href="http://localhost:8080/api/h2-console" rel="noopener ugc nofollow" target="_blank">http://localhost:8080/h2-console</a> and access the database on the web browser. Make sure you have the same JDBC URL, username, and password as in the properties file.</p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt nl nm paragraph-image"><div role="button" tabindex="0" class="nu nv fg nw bg class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on qk op oq or ql ot ou ov qm ox oy oz gv bj">Now the java code is running on port <strong class="og hd">8080</strong>. Now it’s time to look at the React app. The entire React app is under the folder <strong class="og hd"><em class="pg">src/main/ui</em></strong>. You can create with this command <code class="cw sj sk sl rd b">npx create-react-app ui.</code> I am not going to put all the files here you can look at the entire files in the above <a class="af od" href="https://github.com/bbachi/react-java-example" rel="noopener ugc nofollow" target="_blank">Github link or here.</a></p><p id="8263" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">Let’s see some important files here. Here is the service file which calls Java API.</p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt"><div class="se jz l fg"><div class="sf sg l"></div></div><figcaption class="oa fc gr nl nm ob oc be b bf z dt"><strong class="al">UserService.js</strong></figcaption></figure><p id="0109" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">Here is the app component which subscribes to these calls and gets the data from the API.</p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt"><div class="se jz l fg"><div class="sf sg l"></div></div><figcaption class="oa fc gr nl nm ob oc be b bf z dt"><strong class="al">App.js</strong></figcaption></figure><h2 id="95a6" class="rh pn hc be po rn ro dx pr rp rq dz pu on rr rs rt or ru rv rw ov rx ry rz sa bj">Interaction between Angular and Java API</h2><p id="debc" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on qk op oq or ql ot ou ov qm ox oy oz gv bj">In the development phase, the React app is running on port <strong class="og hd">3000</strong> with the help of a create-react-app and Java API running on port <strong class="og hd">8080.</strong></p><p id="d29f" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">There should be some interaction between these two. We can proxy all the API calls to Java API. Create-react-app provides some inbuilt functionality and to tell the development server to proxy any unknown requests to your API server in development, add a <code class="cw sj sk sl rd b">proxy</code> field to your <code class="cw sj sk sl rd b">package.json</code> of the React. Have a look at the below package.json below. Remember you need to put this in the React UI package.json file.</p><figure class="no np nq nr ns nt"><div class="se jz l fg"><div class="sf sg l"></div></div><figcaption class="oa fc gr nl nm ob oc be b bf z dt"><strong class="al">package.json</strong></figcaption></figure><p id="d22d" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">With this in place, all the calls start with <strong class="og hd">/api </strong>will be redirected to <a class="af od" href="http://localhost:3080./" rel="noopener ugc nofollow" target="_blank"><strong class="og hd">http://localhost:8080</strong></a><strong class="og hd"> </strong>where the Java API running.</p><p id="0f1b" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om on oo op oq or os ot ou ov ow ox oy oz gv bj">Once this is configured, you can run the React app on port <strong class="og hd">3000</strong> and java API on <strong class="og hd">8080</strong> still make them work together.</p><pre class="no np nq nr ns rc rd re rf ax rg bj"><span id="5ab0" class="rh pn hc rd b jj ri rj l jy rk">// java API (Terminal 1)<br/>mvn clean install<br/>java -jar target/&lt;war file name&gt;</span><span id="0c6b" class="rh pn hc rd b jj rl rj l jy rk">// React app (Terminal 2)<br/>cd src/mamin/ui<br/>npm start</span></pre></div></div></div><div class="ab ca qo qp qq qr" role="separator"><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu"></span></div><div class="gv gw gx gy gz"><div class="ab ca"><div class="ch bg fx fy fz ga"><h1 id="c654" class="pm pn hc be po pp qw hy pr ps qx ib pu pv qy px py pz qz qb qc qd ra qf qg qh bj">How To Build For Production</h1><p id="24fe" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on qk op oq or ql ot ou ov qm ox oy oz gv bj">As you have seen above, we run the React and Java server on different ports in the development phase. But, when you build the app for production you need to pack your React code with Java and run it on one port. We can use the maven plugin and gulp to package the application for production.</p><blockquote class="sm sn so"><p id="8251" class="oe of pg og b hw oh oi oj hz ok ol om sp oo op oq sq os ot ou sr ow ox oy oz gv bj"><a class="af od" rel="noopener" href="/bb-tutorials-and-thoughts/how-to-build-react-with-java-backend-for-production-72f8634bb067">How To Build React with Java Backend For Production</a></p></blockquote></div></div></div><div class="ab ca qo qp qq qr" role="separator"><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu"></span></div><div class="gv gw gx gy gz"><div class="ab ca"><div class="ch bg fx fy fz ga"><h1 id="63be" class="pm pn hc be po pp qw hy pr ps qx ib pu pv qy px py pz qz qb qc qd ra qf qg qh bj">Summary</h1><ul class=""><li id="5123" class="oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on ss op oq or st ot ou ov su ox oy oz pd pe pf bj">There are so many ways we can build React apps and ship them for production.</li><li id="692c" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj">One way is to build React with Java.</li><li id="8fd7" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj">In the development phase, we can run React and Java on separate ports.</li><li id="6578" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj">The interaction between these two happens with proxying all the calls to API.</li><li id="bbe2" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj">In the production phase, you can build the React app and put all the assets in the build folder and load it with the java code.</li><li id="baba" class="oe of hc og b hw ph oi oj hz pi ol om on pj op oq or pk ot ou ov pl ox oy oz pd pe pf bj">We can package the application for production with a maven plugin and gulp.</li></ul></div></div></div><div class="ab ca qo qp qq qr" role="separator"><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu qv"></span><span class="qs bx bl qt qu"></span></div><div class="gv gw gx gy gz"><div class="ab ca"><div class="ch bg fx fy fz ga"><h1 id="5944" class="pm pn hc be po pp qw hy pr ps qx ib pu pv qy px py pz qz qb qc qd ra qf qg qh bj">Conclusion</h1><p id="4c7a" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oe of hc og b hw qi oi oj hz qj ol om on qk op oq or ql ot ou ov qm ox oy oz gv bj">This is one way of building and shipping React apps. This is really useful when you want to do server-side rendering or you need to do some processing. In future posts, I will discuss more on building for production and deploying strategies.</p></div></div></div></div></section></div></div></article><div class="ab ca"><div class="ch bg fx fy fz ga"></div></div></div><div class="ab ca"><div class="ch bg fx fy fz ga"><div class="sv sw ab jv"><div class="sx ab"><a class="gq ax am ao" rel="noopener follow" href="/tag/react"><div class="sy fg cw
